

```python
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

import numpy as np
import pandas as pd

import panel as pn
pn.extension() # initialize panel notebook extension
```





Testing out panel from https://panel.pyviz.org/getting_started/index.html

First up a basic plotting function which makes a graph figure and returns it without displaying it in the function itself:


```python
def show(m=2.0, n=3.0):
    """makes basic plot, which updates per m and n vars"""
    
    # the data
    x = np.linspace(0, n*np.pi, 500)
    y = np.sin(x**m)
    
    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6,4))
    ax.plot(x, y)
    ax.set_title('A simple chirp')
    plt.close(fig)
    return fig

show()
```




![png](panel_101/panel_101_2_0.png)



Above is the graph I want to be able to tweak visually, so here goes:


```python
pn.interact(show)
```

    function msg_handler(msg) {
      var metadata = msg.metadata;
      var buffers = msg.buffers;
      var msg = msg.content.data;
      if ((metadata.msg_type == "Ready")) {
        if (metadata.content) {
          console.log("Python callback returned following output:", metadata.content);
        }
      } else if (metadata.msg_type == "Error") {
        console.log("Python failed with the following traceback:", metadata.traceback)
      } else {
        
var plot_id = "1469";
if (plot_id in window.PyViz.plot_index) {
  var plot = window.PyViz.plot_index[plot_id];
} else {
  var plot = Bokeh.index[plot_id];
}

if (plot_id in window.PyViz.receivers) {
  var receiver = window.PyViz.receivers[plot_id];
} else if (Bokeh.protocol === undefined) {
  return;
} else {
  var receiver = new Bokeh.protocol.Receiver();
  window.PyViz.receivers[plot_id] = receiver;
}

if ((buffers != undefined) && (buffers.length > 0)) {
  receiver.consume(buffers[0].buffer)
} else {
  receiver.consume(msg)
}

const comm_msg = receiver.message;
if ((comm_msg != null) && (Object.keys(comm_msg.content).length > 0)) {
  plot.model.document.apply_json_patch(comm_msg.content, comm_msg.buffers)
}

      }

      var metadata = msg.metadata;
      var buffers = msg.buffers;
      var msg = msg.content.data;
      if ((metadata.msg_type == "Ready")) {
        if (metadata.content) {
          console.log("Python callback returned following output:", metadata.content);
        }
      } else if (metadata.msg_type == "Error") {
        console.log("Python failed with the following traceback:", metadata.traceback)

```python
from panel import interact

@interact
def show(m=2.0, n=3.0):
    """makes basic plot, which updates per m and n vars"""
    
    # the data
    x = np.linspace(0, n*np.pi, 500)
    y = np.sin(x**m)
    
    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6,4))
    ax.plot(x, y)
    ax.set_title('A simple chirp')
    plt.close(fig)
    return fig

#show()
```
